codex
I’m brute-forcing the small 32x32x8 tile over a tight family of B lane encodings. That’s faster than more blind changes to the fused kernel and should give a concrete pack/unpack pattern to transplant.
exec
/bin/bash -lc "python - <<'PY'
import importlib.util, torch, itertools
spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location('mfma_mod', '/workspace/substrate/test/examples/gemm/amdgpu/test_gemm_mfma.py')
mod = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
spec.loader.exec_module(mod)

def pack4(vals):
    t = torch.tensor(vals, dtype=torch.bfloat16).view(torch.uint16).cpu().numpy().astype('uint32')
    return int(t[0] | (t[1] << 16)), int(t[2] | (t[3] << 16))

def bitrev3(x):
    return ((x & 1) << 2) | (x & 2) | ((x & 4) >> 2)

A = torch.arange(32*8, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda').reshape(32,8).to(torch.bfloat16)
B = (torch.arange(8*32, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda').reshape(8,32) / 10).to(torch.bfloat16)
ref = (A.float() @ B.float()).cpu()
ap = torch.zeros((64,2), dtype=torch.uint32)
for lane in range(64):
    row = lane % 32
    jbase = 0 if lane < 32 else 4
    w0,w1 = pack4(A[row, jbase:jbase+4].cpu().tolist())
    ap[lane,0]=w0; ap[lane,1]=w1
ap = ap.cuda()

best = []
positions = list(itertools.combinations(range(6), 3))
for pos in positions:
    pos = set(pos)
    for krev in [0,1]:
        for grev in [0,1]:
            bp = torch.zeros((64,2), dtype=torch.uint32)
            for k in range(8):
                kk = bitrev3(k) if krev else k
                for grp in range(8):
                    gg = bitrev3(grp) if grev else grp
                    lane = 0
                    kb = [(kk>>i)&1 for i in range(3)]
                    gb = [(gg>>i)&1 for i in range(3)]
                    ki = gi = 0
                    for bit in range(6):
                        if bit in pos:
                            lane |= kb[ki] << bit
                            ki += 1
                        else:
                            lane |= gb[gi] << bit
                            gi += 1
                    cols = slice(grp*4, grp*4+4)
                    w0,w1 = pack4(B[k, cols].cpu().tolist())
                    bp[lane,0]=w0; bp[lane,1]=w1
            C = torch.zeros((64,16), dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
            mod.gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1,1,1),(64,1,1))](ap, bp.cuda(), C)
            out = torch.zeros((32,32), dtype=torch.float32)
            Cc = C.cpu()
            for lane in range(64):
                for acc_idx in range(16):
                    col = lane % 32
                    row = 8*(acc_idx//4) + 4*(lane//32) + (acc_idx%4)
                    out[row,col] = Cc[lane,acc_idx]
            diff = float((out-ref).abs().max())
            best.append((diff, tuple(sorted(pos)), krev, grev))
best.sort(key=lambda x: x[0])
for item in best[:20]:
    print(item)
PY" in /workspace/kernel_benchmark

 POOLED_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // POOL_KERNEL_SIZE
 SCALE_FACTOR = 0.5
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_M = 32
+WAVE_N = 32
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 256
+PARTIAL_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def fused_partial_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    PARTIAL: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, PARTIAL_TILES), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = wave_id >> 1
+    warp_col = wave_id & 1
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    pair_smem = S.make_shared((64, 32), S.f32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    x_bytes = S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.u32)
+    w_bytes = S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.u32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_bytes)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.u32)
+
+    for ko in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = ko * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_local = tid >> 1
+            k_seg = tid & 1
+            row = block_row + row_local
+            byte_offset = S.convert((row * IN_FEATURES + k_base + k_seg * 8) * 2, S.u32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            words = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+            a_wave = row_local >> 5
+            a_lane = row_local & 31
+            word_base = k_seg * 2
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane, word_base + 0] = words[0]
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane, word_base + 1] = words[1]
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane + 32, word_base + 0] = words[2]
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane + 32, word_base + 1] = words[3]
+        else:
+            b_idx = tid - 128
+            k_local = b_idx >> 3
+            col_chunk = b_idx & 7
+            col = block_col + col_chunk * 8
+            byte_offset = S.convert(((k_base + k_local) * OUT_FEATURES + col) * 2, S.u32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            words = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+            b_wave = col_chunk >> 2
+            b_chunk_in_wave = col_chunk & 3
+            word_base = (k_local >> 3) * 2
+            b_row = k_local & 7
+            lane0 = b_row * 8 + b_chunk_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane0, word_base + 0] = words[0]
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane0, word_base + 1] = words[1]
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane1, word_base + 0] = words[2]
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane1, word_base + 1] = words[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    col_idx = block_col + warp_col * WAVE_N + lane_col
+    bias_val = S.convert(BIAS0[col_idx], S.f32)
+    peer_bias = S.shuffle_down(bias_val, 1, 32)
+
+    if lane_col < 31 and (lane_col & 1) == 0:
+        pair_idx = warp_col * 16 + (lane_col >> 1)
+        for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+            row_local = warp_row * WAVE_M + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+            lhs = acc[acc_idx] + bias_val
+            rhs = S.shuffle_down(acc[acc_idx], 1, 32) + peer_bias
+            pair_smem[row_local, pair_idx] = rhs if rhs > lhs else lhs
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < BLOCK_M:
+        total = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for p in S.range(32):
+            total += pair_smem[tid, p]
+        PARTIAL[block_row + tid, S.block_id(0)] = total
+
+

codex
The B packing family search bottoms out at the same error level, so the remaining unknown is the accumulator placement. I’m probing the raw lane/acc output with one-hot tiles to recover the actual `C[lane, acc_idx] -> (row, col)` map for this MFMA primitive.

/bin/bash -lc "python - <<'PY'
import importlib.util, torch
spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location('mfma_mod', '/workspace/substrate/test/examples/gemm/amdgpu/test_gemm_mfma.py')
mod = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
spec.loader.exec_module(mod)

def pack4(vals):
    t = torch.tensor(vals, dtype=torch.bfloat16).view(torch.uint16).cpu().numpy().astype('uint32')
    return int(t[0] | (t[1] << 16)), int(t[2] | (t[3] << 16))

def pack_A(A):
    ap = torch.zeros((64,2), dtype=torch.uint32)
    for lane in range(64):
        row = lane % 32
        jbase = 0 if lane < 32 else 4
        w0,w1 = pack4(A[row, jbase:jbase+4].tolist())
        ap[lane,0]=w0; ap[lane,1]=w1
    return ap.cuda()

def pack_B_alt(B):
    bp = torch.zeros((64,2), dtype=torch.uint32)
    for lane in range(64):
        grp = lane % 8
        k = lane // 8
        cols = slice(grp*4, grp*4+4)
        w0,w1 = pack4(B[k, cols].tolist())
        bp[lane,0]=w0; bp[lane,1]=w1
    return bp.cuda()

for r,c in [(0,0),(0,1),(1,0),(5,7),(31,31)]:
    A = torch.zeros((32,8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    B = torch.zeros((8,32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    A[r,0]=1
    B[0,c]=1
    C = torch.zeros((64,16), dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    mod.gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1,1,1),(64,1,1))](pack_A(A), pack_B_alt(B), C)
    Cc = C.cpu().abs()
    idx = torch.argmax(Cc)
    lane = (idx // 16).item(); acc = (idx % 16).item(); val = Cc.view(-1)[idx].item()
    nz = (Cc > 0.5).nonzero()
    print('target', (r,c), 'top', lane, acc, val, 'count', nz.shape[0], 'first10', nz[:10].tolist())

 POOLED_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // POOL_KERNEL_SIZE
 SCALE_FACTOR = 0.5
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_M = 32
+WAVE_N = 32
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 256
+PARTIAL_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def fused_partial_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    PARTIAL: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, PARTIAL_TILES), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = wave_id >> 1
+    warp_col = wave_id & 1
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    pair_smem = S.make_shared((64, 32), S.f32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    x_bytes = S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.u32)
+    w_bytes = S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.u32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_bytes)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.u32)
+
+    for ko in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = ko * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_local = tid >> 1
+            k_seg = tid & 1
+            row = block_row + row_local
+            byte_offset = S.convert((row * IN_FEATURES + k_base + k_seg * 8) * 2, S.u32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            words = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+            a_wave = row_local >> 5
+            a_lane = row_local & 31
+            word_base = k_seg * 2
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane, word_base + 0] = words[0]
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane, word_base + 1] = words[1]
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane + 32, word_base + 0] = words[2]
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane + 32, word_base + 1] = words[3]
+        else:
+            b_idx = tid - 128
+            k_local = b_idx >> 3
+            col_chunk = b_idx & 7
+            col = block_col + col_chunk * 8
+            byte_offset = S.convert(((k_base + k_local) * OUT_FEATURES + col) * 2, S.u32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            words = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+            b_wave = col_chunk >> 2
+            b_chunk_in_wave = col_chunk & 3
+            word_base = (k_local >> 3) * 2
+            b_row = k_local & 7
+            lane0 = b_row * 8 + b_chunk_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane0, word_base + 0] = words[0]
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane0, word_base + 1] = words[1]
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane1, word_base + 0] = words[2]
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane1, word_base + 1] = words[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    col_idx = block_col + warp_col * WAVE_N + lane_col
+    bias_val = S.convert(BIAS0[col_idx], S.f32)
+    peer_bias = S.shuffle_down(bias_val, 1, 32)
+
+    if lane_col < 31 and (lane_col & 1) == 0:
+        pair_idx = warp_col * 16 + (lane_col >> 1)
+        for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+            row_local = warp_row * WAVE_M + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+            lhs = acc[acc_idx] + bias_val
+            rhs = S.shuffle_down(acc[acc_idx], 1, 32) + peer_bias
+            pair_smem[row_local, pair_idx] = rhs if rhs > lhs else lhs
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < BLOCK_M:
+        total = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for p in S.range(32):
+            total += pair_smem[tid, p]
+        PARTIAL[block_row + tid, S.block_id(0)] = total
+

codex
The one-hot probe shows the current B pack only materializes a strict subset of columns, which narrows the fault further to the intra-fragment B element order / lane grouping. I’m brute-forcing that small local space on the standalone tile instead of perturbing the fused kernel blindly.

/bin/bash -lc "python - <<'PY'
import importlib.util, torch, itertools
spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location('mfma_mod', '/workspace/substrate/test/examples/gemm/amdgpu/test_gemm_mfma.py')
mod = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
spec.loader.exec_module(mod)

def pack4(vals, perm):
    vals = [vals[i] for i in perm]
    t = torch.tensor(vals, dtype=torch.bfloat16).view(torch.uint16).cpu().numpy().astype('uint32')
    return int(t[0] | (t[1] << 16)), int(t[2] | (t[3] << 16))

def pack_A(A):
    ap = torch.zeros((64,2), dtype=torch.uint32)
    for lane in range(64):
        row = lane % 32
        jbase = 0 if lane < 32 else 4
        w0,w1 = pack4(A[row, jbase:jbase+4].tolist(), (0,1,2,3))
        ap[lane,0]=w0; ap[lane,1]=w1
    return ap.cuda()

modes = ['our','alt']
perms = list(itertools.permutations(range(4)))
for mode in modes:
    for perm in perms:
        ok = 0
        for c in range(8):
            A = torch.zeros((32,8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
            B = torch.zeros((8,32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
            A[0,0]=1
            B[0,c]=1
            bp = torch.zeros((64,2), dtype=torch.uint32)
            for lane in range(64):
                if mode=='our':
                    k = lane % 8; grp = lane // 8
                else:
                    grp = lane % 8; k = lane // 8
                cols = slice(grp*4, grp*4+4)
                w0,w1 = pack4(B[k, cols].tolist(), perm)
                bp[lane,0]=w0; bp[lane,1]=w1
            C = torch.zeros((64,16), dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
            mod.gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1,1,1),(64,1,1))](pack_A(A), bp.cuda(), C)
            if float(C.abs().max().cpu()) > 0.5:
                ok += 1
        if ok == 8:
            print('mode', mode, 'perm', perm, 'all first 8 cols active')

 POOLED_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // POOL_KERNEL_SIZE
 SCALE_FACTOR = 0.5
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_M = 32
+WAVE_N = 32
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 256
+PARTIAL_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def fused_partial_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    PARTIAL: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, PARTIAL_TILES), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = wave_id >> 1
+    warp_col = wave_id & 1
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    pair_smem = S.make_shared((64, 32), S.f32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    x_bytes = S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.u32)
+    w_bytes = S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.u32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_bytes)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.u32)
+
+    for ko in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = ko * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_local = tid >> 1
+            k_seg = tid & 1
+            row = block_row + row_local
+            byte_offset = S.convert((row * IN_FEATURES + k_base + k_seg * 8) * 2, S.u32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            words = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+            a_wave = row_local >> 5
+            a_lane = row_local & 31
+            word_base = k_seg * 2
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane, word_base + 0] = words[0]
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane, word_base + 1] = words[1]
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane + 32, word_base + 0] = words[2]
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane + 32, word_base + 1] = words[3]
+        else:
+            b_idx = tid - 128
+            k_local = b_idx >> 3
+            col_chunk = b_idx & 7
+            col = block_col + col_chunk * 8
+            byte_offset = S.convert(((k_base + k_local) * OUT_FEATURES + col) * 2, S.u32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            words = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+            b_wave = col_chunk >> 2
+            b_chunk_in_wave = col_chunk & 3
+            word_base = (k_local >> 3) * 2
+            b_row = k_local & 7
+            lane0 = b_row * 8 + b_chunk_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane0, word_base + 0] = words[0]
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane0, word_base + 1] = words[1]
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane1, word_base + 0] = words[2]
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane1, word_base + 1] = words[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    col_idx = block_col + warp_col * WAVE_N + lane_col
+    bias_val = S.convert(BIAS0[col_idx], S.f32)
+    peer_bias = S.shuffle_down(bias_val, 1, 32)
+
+    if lane_col < 31 and (lane_col & 1) == 0:
+        pair_idx = warp_col * 16 + (lane_col >> 1)
+        for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+            row_local = warp_row * WAVE_M + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+            lhs = acc[acc_idx] + bias_val
+            rhs = S.shuffle_down(acc[acc_idx], 1, 32) + peer_bias
+            pair_smem[row_local, pair_idx] = rhs if rhs > lhs else lhs
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < BLOCK_M:
+        total = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for p in S.range(32):
+            total += pair_smem[tid, p]
+        PARTIAL[block_row + tid, S.block_id(0)] = total
+

+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.")
+
+        self._refresh_static_buffers(x.device, x.dtype)
+        x_in = x.contiguous()
+        partial = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, PARTIAL_TILES), device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
+        y = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+
+        fused_partial_kernel[lambda: ((PARTIAL_TILES, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))](
+            x_in,
+            self._cached_weight_t,
+            self._cached_bias,
+            partial,
+        )
+        fused_reduce_kernel[lambda: ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](partial, y)
         return y

Implemented an MFMA-based tiled kernel in [output_model_new.py](/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p55/optimization_rounds/round1/output_model_new.py), using `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32`, `raw_buffer_load_x4`, LDS staging, a 2x2 wave grid, cached transposed weights/bias, and a separate reduction kernel.

I also ran the exact required evaluation command. The kernel compiles, but it does not pass correctness yet: the latest `debug_eval.jsonl` still reports `correctness: false` with `max_difference: 480` and `avg_difference: 456`. The remaining issue is in the MFMA operand/output lane mapping rather than launch or reduction structure.

 POOLED_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // POOL_KERNEL_SIZE
 SCALE_FACTOR = 0.5
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_M = 32
+WAVE_N = 32
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 256
+PARTIAL_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def fused_partial_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    PARTIAL: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, PARTIAL_TILES), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = wave_id >> 1
+    warp_col = wave_id & 1
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    pair_smem = S.make_shared((64, 32), S.f32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    x_bytes = S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2, S.u32)
+    w_bytes = S.convert(IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2, S.u32)
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_bytes)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.u32)
+
+    for ko in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = ko * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_local = tid >> 1
+            k_seg = tid & 1
+            row = block_row + row_local
+            byte_offset = S.convert((row * IN_FEATURES + k_base + k_seg * 8) * 2, S.u32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            words = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+            a_wave = row_local >> 5
+            a_lane = row_local & 31
+            word_base = k_seg * 2
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane, word_base + 0] = words[0]
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane, word_base + 1] = words[1]
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane + 32, word_base + 0] = words[2]
+            a_smem[a_wave, a_lane + 32, word_base + 1] = words[3]
+        else:
+            b_idx = tid - 128
+            k_local = b_idx >> 3
+            col_chunk = b_idx & 7
+            col = block_col + col_chunk * 8
+            byte_offset = S.convert(((k_base + k_local) * OUT_FEATURES + col) * 2, S.u32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            words = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+            b_wave = col_chunk >> 2
+            b_chunk_in_wave = col_chunk & 3
+            word_base = (k_local >> 3) * 2
+            b_row = k_local & 7
+            lane0 = b_row * 8 + b_chunk_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane0, word_base + 0] = words[0]
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane0, word_base + 1] = words[1]
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane1, word_base + 0] = words[2]
+            b_smem[b_wave, lane1, word_base + 1] = words[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    col_idx = block_col + warp_col * WAVE_N + lane_col
+    bias_val = S.convert(BIAS0[col_idx], S.f32)
+    peer_bias = S.shuffle_down(bias_val, 1, 32)
+
+    if lane_col < 31 and (lane_col & 1) == 0:
+        pair_idx = warp_col * 16 + (lane_col >> 1)
+        for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+            row_local = warp_row * WAVE_M + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+            lhs = acc[acc_idx] + bias_val
+            rhs = S.shuffle_down(acc[acc_idx], 1, 32) + peer_bias
+            pair_smem[row_local, pair_idx] = rhs if rhs > lhs else lhs
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < BLOCK_M:
+        total = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for p in S.range(32):
+            total += pair_smem[tid, p]
+        PARTIAL[block_row + tid, S.block_id(0)] = total
+
